 This boom of the market is a story of elevating the Sensex and Nifty due to buying in select stocks
 yahi kaaran he ki nifti jab 12,000 ke jaadui aankade kii choukhat par khadaa he tab nifti kaa hi realty index apane ucchtam str se 85 fisadi neeche he

 metal or auto kaa haal bhi bahut acha nahin
 Both these indices are also down 37 and 31 percent respectively
 arthvyavastha kii gatividhiyaan ko darshane vaale tamaam aankade (kor sector, piemi index, vaahan bikri, ghar bikri, iypi) abhi aarthik vikaas kii raftaar main jald kisi teji kii ummid nahin jataa rahe hai
 In such a situation, the running of the market definitely confuses investors because if the economy is so bad then why are the stock markets considered to be the mirror of the economy so happy? To solve this problem, two steps have to be taken
 pehla, sarkaar kii ore se kii gai korporate tex main katautee
 This relief, which was put in the hands of corporates by the government, inflated the profits of the companies
 yah bhi tab hua jab bikri sikud rahi he
 The company's profits were actually due to tax concessions
 yah riyaayat unhen arthvyavastha main nivesh badhaane kii manshaa ke saath di gai
 However, the answer remains to find the question that if consumption is shrinking, then who should go for new investment? Because investment comes only by holding the tail of consumption
 doosraa sira he bazaar main aa rahi sasti nakadi
 After the cut in interest rates by the Federal Reserve, the way for foreign investors to continue to get cheaper capital for a long time
 yahi kaaran he videshi niveshkon ne aktubar main 14,600 karod rupye se zyada kii kharidari kii he, yah kharidari aage bhi jari rahane kii ummid he
 Apart from this, the huge investment coming in the stock market through mutual funds through SIP is giving rise to the boom
 trade war ke thamane kii ummid, kendriya bank kii ore se byaaj dar main katautee bhi bazaar ke nazariye se achche sanket hai
 For the market to be all-round and fast, it is necessary to improve the domestic economy, so that the profits of the companies should be based on growth consumption rather than abruptly due to any tax relief
 is teji main kisi badi kharidari se parhez kii salaah rahegi
 When the market falls, select stocks should be bought slowly
 iske alaava agar aap mutual funds ke raste bazaar kaa rukh karte hai to kisi bhi str par kharidari shuru kar sakate hai

 2

 5

 8
